    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined

    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }

    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range

    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

    \section{Predict with fixed Value}\label{predict-with-fixed-value}

\subsection{1. Default Values}\label{default-values}

About 80\% of the training data are: 0 0 0
(forward\_count,comment\_count,like\_count) and also, 96\% of uid in
predict dataset is present in train dataset, for remaining 4\% which are
new, we need some default values. inspired by this, we try some fixed
value for all uid:

    \subsubsection{Function to take Fixed FCL Values, Give Accuracy and
Generate Predicted
FCL}\label{function-to-take-fixed-fcl-values-give-accuracy-and-generate-predicted-fcl}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor} }]:} \PY{n+nd}{@runTime}
        \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{predict\PYZus{}with\PYZus{}fixed\PYZus{}value}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{comment}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{like}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{submission}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        	\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} type check}
        	\PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{isinstance}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n+nb}{isinstance}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n+nb}{isinstance}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        		\PY{k}{pass}
        	\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        		\PY{k}{raise} \PY{n+ne}{TypeError}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{forward,comment,like should be type }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{int}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        	
        	\PY{n}{traindata}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{testdata} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{loadData}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        	
        	\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}score on the training set}
        	\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{traindata}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{forward\PYZus{}count}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{comment\PYZus{}count}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{like\PYZus{}count}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}
        	\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{fp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{cp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{lp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{comment}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{like}
        	\PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Score on the training set:}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}0:.2f\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{precision}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        	
        	\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}predict on the test data with fixed value, generate submission file}
        	\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{submission}\PY{p}{:}
        		\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{testdata}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{u\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{m\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}
        		\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{fp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{cp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{lp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{comment}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{like}
        		
        		\PY{n}{result} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        		\PY{n}{filename} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{weibo\PYZus{}predict\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{.txt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{comment}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{like}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iterrows}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        			\PY{n}{result}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}0\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}t}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}1\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}t}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}2\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}3\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}4\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{n}{f} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{writelines}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{result}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{close}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{generate submission file }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \subsection{2. UID Statistics (Mean, Max, Min,
Median)}\label{uid-statistics-mean-max-min-median}

Another wise solution is to predict respectively with uid's
statistics(E.g mean,median) , their score on the training data: \#\#\#
Function to take Statistical Factor, Give Accuracy and Generate
Predicted FCL

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor} }]:} \PY{n+nd}{@runTime}	
        \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{predict\PYZus{}with\PYZus{}stat}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stat}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{median}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{submission}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        	\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{	stat:}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{		string}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{		min,max,mean,median}
        \PY{l+s+sd}{	\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        	\PY{n}{stat\PYZus{}dic} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{genUidStat}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        	\PY{n}{traindata}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{testdata} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{loadData}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        	
        	\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}get stat for each uid}
        	\PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{comment}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{like} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        	\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{uid} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{traindata}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{u\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}
        		\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{uid} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{stat\PYZus{}dic}\PY{p}{:}
        			\PY{n}{forward}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stat\PYZus{}dic}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{uid}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{forward\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{stat}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

        			\PY{n}{like}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stat\PYZus{}dic}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{uid}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{like\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{stat}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

        	\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}score on the training set}

        	\PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Score on the training set:}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}0:.2f\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{precision}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}real\PYZus{}pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsection{The data is split into 400 chunks and translated
individually and concatenated
back}\label{the-data-is-split-into-400-chunks-and-translated-individually-and-concatenated-back}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor} }]:} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{j} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{400}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{filename}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{G:}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{concatfiles}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{.txt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
            \PY{n}{transname}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{G:}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{translated}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ts}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{.zh\PYZhy{}CN.en.txt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{transname}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read\PYZus{}csv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{t}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read\PYZus{}csv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{transname}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{sep}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{5A09}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{frames} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{t}\PY{p}{]}
        
            \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{concat}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{frames}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{join}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{outer}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ignore\PYZus{}index}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{keys}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{levels}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{names}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{verify\PYZus{}integrity}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{copy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{n}{stem} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}

            \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{Exception} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{n}{nltk\PYZus{}tokens} \PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{tokens} 
            \PY{n}{lem} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Next find the roots of the word}
            \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{w} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{nltk\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{p}{:}
                    \PY{n}{l}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{wordnet\PYZus{}lemmatizer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lemmatize}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{w}\PY{p}{)}
                    \PY{n}{lem}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{l}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{lem}
            \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{Exception} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{tokens}
\end{Verbatim}

    \section{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-MODEL
BUILDING-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-}\label{model-building-----------------}

    \section{BOW}\label{bow}

Contribution: Apoorva Malemath

    We convert text to a numerical representation called a feature vector. A
feature vector can be as simple as a list of numbers.

The bag-of-words model is one of the feature extraction algorithms for
text.

1.The first step in this model is defining the vocabulary

2.The second step is to convert sentences into a frequency vector based
on the vocabulary.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor} }]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Reading data from document}
        \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{pandas} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{pd}
        \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}pre}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read\PYZus{}csv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{E:}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{DMA\PYZus{}PRE}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{PREPROCESSED.csv}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read\PYZus{}csv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{E:}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{DMA\PYZus{}PRE}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{PREPROCESSED.csv}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}Adjustments to be done for the data}
        \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{content}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{content}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{str}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{content}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{content}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{str}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{n}{ignore\PYZus{}words} \PY{o}{=}             \PY{n}{words} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{[\PYZca{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{w]}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{n}{sentence}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}nltk.word\PYZus{}tokenize(sentence)}
            \PY{n}{words\PYZus{}cleaned} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{w}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lower}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{w} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{words} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{w} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{ignore\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{words\PYZus{}cleaned}    
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}function which returns feature vector}
        \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{bagofwords}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sentence}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{words}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{sentence\PYZus{}words} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{extract\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sentence}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} frequency word count}
            \PY{n}{bag} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{zeros}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{words}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{sw} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{sentence\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{word} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{words}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{word} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{sw}\PY{p}{:} 
                        \PY{n}{bag}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
                        
            \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{bag}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \section{Model : (Factors: Media, Length, Emoji, Median,Polarity) with
Ridge
regression}\label{model-factors-media-length-emoji-medianpolarity-with-ridge-regression}

\subsubsection{Ridge regression is used to prevent multicollinearity
among variables by shrinking the
parameters}\label{ridge-regression-is-used-to-prevent-multicollinearity-among-variables-by-shrinking-the-parameters}

        		\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{uid} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{testdata}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{u\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{:}

        				\PY{n}{forward}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{uid\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{uid}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        				\PY{n}{comment}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{uid\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{uid}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        				\PY{n}{like}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{uid\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{uid}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        			\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        				\PY{n}{forward}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
        				\PY{n}{comment}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
        				\PY{n}{like}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{fp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{cp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{lp}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{forward}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{comment}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{like}
        		
        		\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}generate submission file}
        		\PY{n}{result} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        		\PY{n}{filename} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{weibo\PYZus{}predict\PYZus{}search.txt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
        		\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iterrows}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        			\PY{n}{result}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}0\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}t}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}1\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}t}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}2\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}3\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{,}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}4\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{n}{f} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        		\PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{writelines}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{result}\PY{p}{)}

        		\PY{n+nb}{print} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{generate submission file }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{filename}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{predict\PYZus{}by\PYZus{}search}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \section{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-Conclusions-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-}\label{conclusions---------------------------------------------------}

    We built models to predict the number of forwards, comments and likes
for a weibo. We followed an iterative KDD process to refine the
pre-processing of data and improve the performance of model. As the
crucial part of our data is text, we apply text preprocessing techniques
namely removal of noise, stop words, stemming and lemmatization.

We found that using the algorithmic approach where we defined the best
possible value for each user based the UID yielded good result. The
model used statistical factors and yielded a score of 29.82\% and got a
rank of 218 on leaderboard.

Also computing polarity of the text and performing a min max
normalization on it yielded a score of 78.92\% on the cross validation.
